This file contains the list of potential API break. A pattern was used to look through all your files and note the spots where you might have a problem. Not everything here is broken./ns\.workForCompany/g
workForCompany argument companyName is now not-optional.

	/ns/workForCompany.js
		Line 7 const result = await ns.workForCompany(...args);


/ns\.getScriptExpGain/g
getScriptExpGain with 0 argument no longer returns the sum of all scripts. Use getTotalScriptExpGain

	/ns/getScriptExpGain.js
		Line 7 const result = await ns.getScriptExpGain(...args);


/ns\.getScriptExpGain/g
getScriptIncome with 0 argument no longer returns the sum of all scripts. Use getTotalScriptIncome

	/ns/getScriptExpGain.js
		Line 7 const result = await ns.getScriptExpGain(...args);


/ns\.scp/g
scp arguments were switch, it is now scp(files, destination, optionally_source). If you were using 2 argument (not 3) this doesn't affect you.

	/tools/rent.js
		Line 43 await ns.scp("/cache/augment/serverInfo.js", result);
	/farm/smart/smart-setup.js
		Line 20 if(weakHost != "home") await ns.scp(weakScript, "home", weakHost);
		Line 49 if(hosts[0] != "home") await ns.scp(scripts.hackScript, hosts[0]);
		Line 50 if(hosts[1] != "home") await ns.scp(scripts.growScript, hosts[1]);
		Line 51 if(hosts[2] != "home") await ns.scp(scripts.weakScript, hosts[2]);
	/lib/alloc.js
		Line 102 await ns.scp(script, host);
		Line 114 for(const file of files) await ns.scp(file, target);
	/old/mastermind.js
		Line 81 if(host != "home") await ns.scp(trainingScript, host);
		Line 132 await ns.scp(trainingScript, gigaServer);
	/science/test-exp-grind.js
		Line 36 await ns.scp(script, host);
	/lib/cache.js
		Line 132 if(host != "home") await ns.scp(filename, host);
	/old/prepare-servers.js

	/old/mastermind2.js
		Line 73 if(host != "home") await ns.scp(farmScript, host);
	newFarm.js

	/ns/scp.js
